It's open source with open pricing. You pick from 500+ models, switch between them mid-task, and pay the model provider's rate with zero markup. No API keys required to start.</p>\n<div class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"><h3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\">Installation</h3><a id=\"user-content-installation\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Installation\" href=\"#installation\"><svg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a></div>\n<p dir=\"auto\">Pick where you want to run Kilo.</p>\n<details open=\"\">\n<summary><strong>VS Code</strong></summary>\n<br>\n<p dir=\"auto\">Install the Kilo Code extension directly, or grab it from the <a href=\"https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=kilocode.Kilo-Code\" rel=\"nofollow\">VS Code Marketplace</a>. Create an account and you'll have access to 500+ models including GPT-5.5, Claude Opus 4.7, Claude Sonnet 4.6, and Gemini 3.1 Pro Preview, all at provider pricing.</p>\n</details>\n<details href=\"https://app.kilo.ai/cloud\" rel=\"nofollow\">app.kilo.ai/cloud</a>.</p>\n</details>\n<details>\n<summary><strong>Code Reviews</strong></summary>\n<br>\n<p dir=\"auto\">Set up automated AI code reviews on your pull requests at <a href=\"https://app.kilo.ai/code-reviews\" href=\"https://app.kilo.ai/claw\" rel=\"nofollow\">app.kilo.ai/claw</a>.</p>\n</details>\n<details>\n<summary>Install the CLI from GitHub Releases (binaries)</summary>\n<p dir=\"auto\">Download the latest binary from the <a href=\"https://github.com/Kilo-Org/kilocode/releases\">Releases page</a>.</p>\n<markdown-accessiblity-table data-catalyst=\"\"><table>\n<thead>\n<tr>\n<th>Platform</th>\n<th>Asset</th>\n</tr>\n</thead>\n<tbody>\n<tr>\n<td>Windows (most PCs)</td>\n<td><code>kilo-windows-x64.zip</code></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>macOS (Apple Silicon)</td>\n<td><code>kilo-darwin-arm64.zip</code></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>macOS CPUs without AVX. <code>musl</code> is the statically linked build for Alpine or minimal Docker images without glibc. <code>kilo-vscode-*.vsix</code> is the VS Code extension package, not the CLI. <code>Source code</code> archives are for building from source.</p>\n</details>\n<div class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"><h3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\">Agents</h3><a id=\"user-content-agents\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Agents\" href=\"#agents\"><svg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a></div>\n<p dir=\"auto\">Kilo ships with specialized agents you switch between depending on the task. You can also build your own custom agents.</p>\n<ul dir=\"auto\">\n<li><strong>Code</strong> - The default. Implements and edits code from natural language.</li>\n<li><strong>Plan</strong> - Designs architecture and writes implementation plans before any code gets written.</li>\n<li><strong>Ask</strong> - Answers questions about your codebase without touching any files.</li>\n<li><strong>Debug</strong> - Troubleshoots and traces issues.</li>\n<li><strong>Review</strong> - Reviews your changes and surfaces issues across performance, security, style, and test coverage.</li>\n</ul>\n<p dir=\"auto\">Learn more about <a href=\"https://kilo.ai/docs/code-with-ai/agents/using-agents\" rel=\"nofollow\">agents and custom agents</a>.</p>\n<div class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"><h3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\">What it does</h3><a id=\"user-content-what-it-does\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: What it does\" href=\"#what-it-does\"><svg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a></div>\n<ul dir=\"auto\">\n<li><strong>Code generation</strong> from natural language, across multiple files.</li>\n<li><strong>Inline autocomplete</strong> with ghost-text suggestions and tab to accept.</li>\n<li><strong>Self-checking</strong> so the agent reviews and corrects its own work.</li>\n<li><strong>Terminal and browser control</strong> to run commands and automate the web.</li>\n<li><strong>MCP marketplace</strong> to find and wire up MCP servers that extend what the agent can do.</li>\n<li><strong>500+ models</strong> with mid-task switching, so you can match latency, cost, and reasoning to the job.</li>\n</ul>\n<div class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"><h3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\">Autonomous Mode (CI/CD)</h3><a
